class TestMCPToolsBasic:

    async def test_tool_functions_importable(self):
        """Test that all MCP tool functions can be imported."""
        try:
            # Import inside test to avoid module loading issues
            import sys
            sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), '..', '..', 'src'))
            
            import crawl4ai_mcp
            
            # Check that key functions exist
            assert hasattr(crawl4ai_mcp, 'crawl_single_page')
            assert hasattr(crawl4ai_mcp, 'smart_crawl_url')
            assert hasattr(crawl4ai_mcp, 'perform_rag_query')
            assert hasattr(crawl4ai_mcp, 'get_available_sources')
            assert hasattr(crawl4ai_mcp, 'search_code_examples')
            
        except ImportError as e:
            pytest.skip(f"Could not import MCP module: {e}")
    
    @pytest.mark.asyncio
    async def test_crawl_single_page_function_signature(self):
        """Test that crawl_single_page has the expected signature."""
        try:
            import sys
            sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), '..', '..', 'src'))
            
            from crawl4ai_mcp import crawl_single_page
            import inspect
            
            sig = inspect.signature(crawl_single_page)
            params = list(sig.parameters.keys())
            
            # Should have at least ctx and url parameters
            assert 'ctx' in params
            assert 'url' in params
            
        except ImportError as e:
            pytest.skip(f"Could not import crawl_single_page: {e}")
    
    @pytest.mark.asyncio
    async def test_perform_rag_query_function_signature(self):
        """Test that perform_rag_query has the expected signature."""
        try:
            import sys
            sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), '..', '..', 'src'))
            
            from crawl4ai_mcp import perform_rag_query
            import inspect
            
            sig = inspect.signature(perform_rag_query)
            params = list(sig.parameters.keys())
            
            # Should have at least ctx and query parameters
            assert 'ctx' in params
            assert 'query' in params
            
        except ImportError as e:
            pytest.skip(f"Could not import perform_rag_query: {e}")

<file path="tests\unit\test_utils.py.disabled">
"""Unit tests for the utils module."""

import pytest
from unittest.mock import AsyncMock, MagicMock, patch
import asyncio

# Import the functions to test
import sys
import os
sys.path.insert(0, os.path.join(os.path.dirname(__file__), '..', '..', 'src'))

from utils import (
    create_embedding,
    create_embeddings_batch,
    add_documents_to_supabase,
    search_documents,
    extract_code_blocks,
    add_code_examples_to_supabase,
    generate_code_example_summary,
)


class TestExtractCodeBlocks:
    """Test the extract_code_blocks function."""
    
    def test_extract_python_code(self):
        """Test extraction of Python code blocks."""
        markdown_content = """
        Here's a Python example:
        ```python
        def hello():
            print("Hello, World!")
        ```
        
        And some text after.
        """
        
        code_blocks = extract_code_blocks(markdown_content, min_length=0)
        
        assert len(code_blocks) >= 1
        # Check if any block contains Python code
        python_found = any('def hello():' in block.get('code', '') for block in code_blocks)
        assert python_found
    
    def test_extract_multiple_languages(self):
        """Test extraction of multiple programming languages."""
        content = """
        Python:
        ```python
        print("Hello")
        ```
        
        JavaScript:
        ```javascript
        console.log("Hello");
        ```
        """
        
        code_blocks = extract_code_blocks(content, min_length=0)
        
        assert len(code_blocks) >= 2
    
    def test_no_code_blocks(self):
        """Test content with no code blocks."""
        content = "This is just regular text with no code examples."
        
        code_blocks = extract_code_blocks(content, min_length=0)
        assert len(code_blocks) == 0
    
    def test_min_length_filter(self):
        """Test filtering by minimum code length."""
        content = """
        Short code:
        ```python
        x = 1
        ```
        
        Long code:
        ```python
        def complex_function():
            # This is a longer code block
            for i in range(100):
                print(f"Processing item {i}")
                if i % 10 == 0:
                    print("Checkpoint reached")
            return "Done"
        ```
        """
        
        # Test with high minimum length
        long_blocks = extract_code_blocks(content, min_length=100)
        short_blocks = extract_code_blocks(content, min_length=0)
        
        assert len(short_blocks) >= len(long_blocks)


class TestCreateEmbedding:
    """Test the create_embedding function."""
    
    @patch.dict(os.environ, {"OPENAI_API_KEY": "test_key"})
    def test_create_single_embedding(self, mock_openai_client):
        """Test creating embedding for a single text."""
        with patch('utils.openai') as mock_openai:
            mock_openai.embeddings.create.return_value = MagicMock(
                data=[MagicMock(embedding=[0.1] * 1536)]
            )
            
            embedding = create_embedding("Test text")
            
            assert len(embedding) == 1536
            assert all(isinstance(x, float) for x in embedding)
            mock_openai.embeddings.create.assert_called()
    
    @patch.dict(os.environ, {"OPENAI_API_KEY": "test_key"})
    def test_create_embedding_error_handling(self, mock_openai_client):
        """Test error handling in embedding creation."""
        with patch('utils.openai') as mock_openai:
            mock_openai.embeddings.create.side_effect = Exception("API Error")
            
            # Should handle error gracefully
            embedding = create_embedding("Test text")
            
            # Should return fallback embedding
            assert isinstance(embedding, list)
            assert len(embedding) == 1536
            assert all(x == 0.0 for x in embedding)  # Fallback is zeros


class TestCreateEmbeddingsBatch:
    """Test the create_embeddings_batch function."""
    
    @patch.dict(os.environ, {"OPENAI_API_KEY": "test_key"})
    def test_create_batch_embeddings(self, mock_openai_client):
        """Test creating embeddings for multiple texts."""
        with patch('utils.openai') as mock_openai:
            # Mock batch response
            mock_openai.embeddings.create.return_value = MagicMock(
                data=[
                    MagicMock(embedding=[0.1] * 1536),
                    MagicMock(embedding=[0.2] * 1536),
                    MagicMock(embedding=[0.3] * 1536),
                ]
            )
            
            texts = ["Text 1", "Text 2", "Text 3"]
            embeddings = create_embeddings_batch(texts)
            
            assert len(embeddings) == 3
            assert all(len(emb) == 1536 for emb in embeddings)
    
    def test_empty_text_list(self, mock_openai_client):
        """Test handling of empty text list."""
        embeddings = create_embeddings_batch([])
        assert embeddings == []


class TestAddDocumentsToSupabase:
    """Test the add_documents_to_supabase function."""
    
    @pytest.mark.asyncio
    async def test_add_documents_success(self, mock_supabase_client, sample_document_chunks):
        """Test successful addition of documents to Supabase."""
        with patch('utils.get_supabase_client', return_value=mock_supabase_client):
            mock_supabase_client.table.return_value.insert.return_value.execute.return_value = MagicMock(
                data=sample_document_chunks
            )
            
            # Prepare document data in expected format
            documents = []
            for chunk in sample_document_chunks:
                documents.append({
                    'content': chunk['content'],
                    'source': chunk['source'],
                    'embedding': chunk['embedding'],
                    'metadata': chunk['metadata']
                })
            
            result = await add_documents_to_supabase(documents)
            
            assert result is True
            mock_supabase_client.table.assert_called_with('crawled_pages')
    
    @pytest.mark.asyncio
    async def test_add_documents_failure(self, mock_supabase_client):
        """Test handling of storage failure."""
        with patch('utils.get_supabase_client', return_value=mock_supabase_client):
            mock_supabase_client.table.return_value.insert.return_value.execute.side_effect = Exception("DB Error")
            
            documents = [{"content": "test", "metadata": {}, "embedding": [0.1] * 1536, "source": "test"}]
            result = await add_documents_to_supabase(documents)
            
            assert result is False


class TestSearchDocuments:
    """Test the search_documents function."""
    
    @pytest.mark.asyncio
    async def test_search_documents_success(self, mock_supabase_client):
        """Test successful document search."""
        with patch('utils.get_supabase_client', return_value=mock_supabase_client):
            mock_supabase_client.rpc.return_value.execute.return_value = MagicMock(
                data=[{"content": "test result", "similarity": 0.8, "source": "https://example.com"}]
            )
            
            results = await search_documents(
                query_embedding=[0.1] * 1536,
                limit=5,
                similarity_threshold=0.7
            )
            
            assert len(results) >= 0
            mock_supabase_client.rpc.assert_called()
    
    @pytest.mark.asyncio
    async def test_search_documents_with_source_filter(self, mock_supabase_client):
        """Test document search with source filtering."""
        with patch('utils.get_supabase_client', return_value=mock_supabase_client):
            mock_supabase_client.rpc.return_value.execute.return_value = MagicMock(
                data=[{"content": "filtered result", "similarity": 0.9, "source": "https://example.com"}]
            )
            
            results = await search_documents(
                query_embedding=[0.1] * 1536,
                limit=5,
                source_filter="example.com"
            )
            
            assert isinstance(results, list)


class TestGenerateCodeExampleSummary:
    """Test the generate_code_example_summary function."""
    
    @pytest.mark.asyncio
    async def test_generate_summary(self, mock_openai_client):
        """Test generating summary for code example."""
        with patch('utils.openai', mock_openai_client):
            mock_openai_client.chat.completions.create.return_value = MagicMock(
                choices=[MagicMock(message=MagicMock(content="A simple hello world function"))]
            )
            
            code = "def hello():\n    print('Hello, World!')"
            summary = await generate_code_example_summary(code, "Introduction", "End of example")
            
            assert isinstance(summary, str)
            assert len(summary) > 0
            mock_openai_client.chat.completions.create.assert_called_once()
    
    @pytest.mark.asyncio
    async def test_generate_summary_error(self, mock_openai_client):
        """Test error handling in summary generation."""
        with patch('utils.openai', mock_openai_client):
            mock_openai_client.chat.completions.create.side_effect = Exception("API Error")
            
            code = "def hello():\n    print('Hello, World!')"
            
            try:
                summary = await generate_code_example_summary(code, "", "")
                # Should handle error gracefully
                assert summary is None or isinstance(summary, str)
            except Exception:
                # Exception is also acceptable
                pass
